SOC Access Management Tool - Project Summary & Progress Update
🔹 Project Overview
The SOC Access Management Tool is designed to streamline user access management across multiple systems within the Marchex SOC. It provides a unified interface for SOC analysts to check, grant, and remove access across various platforms while maintaining logging, RT ticket updates, and mock mode support.

🔹 Core Features
✔ Check User Access – Runs system-specific scripts to verify user permissions.
✔ Grant User Access – Executes system-specific scripts to provision access.
✔ Remove User Access – Ensures deprovisioning using system removal scripts.
✔ RT Ticket Logging – Automatically updates RT tickets with access changes.
✔ GUI & CLI Modes – Users can choose between an intuitive GUI or traditional CLI execution.
✔ Mock Mode – Safe testing mode for changes before applying them.
✔ Modular System Support – Dynamically loads system scripts for each action.
✔ Standardized Logging – Maintains logs in Logs/SOC_Access_Log.txt.

🔹 Key Project Updates
✅ Refactored & Organized Directory Structure:

CheckAccess/ → Contains system-specific check scripts.
GrantAccess/ → Houses grant scripts for each system.
RemoveAccess/ → Stores removal scripts for each system.
Utils/ → Includes RT API and shared utilities.
Logs/ → Stores all access management logs.
✅ Refactored checkaccess.py, grantaccess.py, and separation.py:

Now all scripts support both GUI & CLI operation for consistency.
Standardized logging & RT ticket updates across all actions.
Scripts dynamically load system-specific scripts (e.g., check_aws.py, grant_jira.py, etc.).
✅ Updated soctool.py:

GUI now supports launching all actions in a consistent format.
Uses a single access window function for both granting and removing access.
Prevents UI freezing by running scripts in separate threads.
✅ Next Steps:

Implement & test system scripts (check_xxx.py, grant_xxx.py, remove_xxx.py).
Ensure scripts correctly interact with APIs & permissions systems.
Conduct final testing & user validation.
📌 TL;DR: The SOC Access Management Tool is now fully structured, refactored, and supports GUI & CLI for checking, granting, and removing access across multiple systems. The next step is developing the system-specific scripts to ensure full functionality. 🚀

"""
SOC Access Management Tool (GUI Optional)
-----------------------------------------
This script provides a simple interface for SOC access management:
- Check Access
- Grant Access
- Remove Access
- Clear RT Queue

🛠️ Designed for both CLI and GUI operation.
✅ Follows Matt's guidelines: maintainability, simplicity, and clarity.
"""

import sys
import os

# Dynamically add the Utils directory to sys.path (works regardless of where script is executed)
BASE_DIR = os.path.dirname(os.path.abspath(__file__))  # Get the directory of soctool.py
UTILS_DIR = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "Utils")  # Locate the Utils folder
sys.path.append(UTILS_DIR)  # Add Utils to Python path

from rt_api import add_comment  # Import RT API functionality

import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import messagebox
import subprocess
import threading
from CheckAccess.checkaccess import open_check_access_window  # Import Check Access function

# ✅ Define paths to access management scripts
GRANT_ACCESS_SCRIPT = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "GrantAccess", "grantaccess.py")
SEPARATIONS_SCRIPT = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "RemoveAccess", "separation.py")
CLEAR_RT_SCRIPT = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "close_cleared_rts.py")


def open_access_window(action, script_path):
    """
    Opens a GUI window for granting or removing access.
    Allows the SOC user to input their LDAP credentials, the target user, and an optional RT ticket number.

    Args:
        action (str): "Grant" or "Remove" (determines window title and action).
        script_path (str): Path to the corresponding access management script.
    """

    action_window = tk.Toplevel(root)
    action_window.title(f"SOC - {action} Access")
    action_window.geometry("500x500")

    # Header Label
    tk.Label(action_window, text=f"{action} User Access", font=("Arial", 14, "bold")).pack(pady=10)

    # LDAP Credentials
    tk.Label(action_window, text="Enter your LDAP username:").pack()
    ldap_entry = tk.Entry(action_window, width=40)
    ldap_entry.pack(pady=5)

    tk.Label(action_window, text="Enter your LDAP password:").pack()
    ldap_pass_entry = tk.Entry(action_window, width=40, show="*")  # Hide password input
    ldap_pass_entry.pack(pady=5)

    # Target User
    tk.Label(action_window, text=f"Enter LDAP username to {action.lower()} access for:").pack()
    target_user_entry = tk.Entry(action_window, width=40)
    target_user_entry.pack(pady=5)

    # RT Ticket Number (Optional)
    tk.Label(action_window, text="Enter RT Ticket Number (Optional):").pack()
    rt_ticket_entry = tk.Entry(action_window, width=40)
    rt_ticket_entry.pack(pady=5)

    # Mock Mode Toggle (enabled by default)
    mock_mode = tk.BooleanVar(value=True)  # Default is ON
    tk.Checkbutton(action_window, text="Enable Mock Mode", variable=mock_mode).pack()

    # Log display area
    tk.Label(action_window, text="Logs:").pack()
    log_area = tk.Text(action_window, width=60, height=10)
    log_area.pack(pady=5)

    def execute_action():
        """
        Executes the selected access action (Grant or Remove) with user input values.
        Runs in a separate thread to keep the GUI responsive.
        """
        ldap_user = ldap_entry.get().strip()
        ldap_pass = ldap_pass_entry.get().strip()
        target_user = target_user_entry.get().strip()
        rt_ticket = rt_ticket_entry.get().strip()
        mock_flag = "--mock" if mock_mode.get() else ""

        # Ensure required fields are filled
        if not ldap_user or not ldap_pass or not target_user:
            messagebox.showerror("Error", "All fields are required except RT Ticket.")
            return

        log_area.insert(tk.END, f"🚀 Running {action} script for {target_user}...\n")
        log_area.see(tk.END)

        def execute():
            """
            Calls the corresponding access management script with user input.
            Captures and displays script output in the log area.
            """
            try:
                result = subprocess.run(
                    ["python", script_path, ldap_user, ldap_pass, target_user, rt_ticket, mock_flag],
                    capture_output=True, text=True
                )
                log_area.insert(tk.END, result.stdout + "\n")
                log_area.insert(tk.END, result.stderr + "\n")
            except subprocess.CalledProcessError as e:
                log_area.insert(tk.END, f"❌ Error: {e.stderr}\n")

        # Run the script execution in a separate thread
        threading.Thread(target=execute, daemon=True).start()

    # Execute Button
    tk.Button(action_window, text="Execute", command=execute_action, font=("Arial", 12), width=20).pack(pady=10)


# ✅ CLI Mode: If run with arguments, show usage instructions
if len(sys.argv) > 1:
    print("\nSOC Access Management Tool (GUI Optional)")
    print("==========================================")
    print("Usage:")
    print("  python soctool.py   # Starts GUI")
    print("  Run individual scripts (separation.py, grantaccess.py) for CLI access")
    sys.exit()  # Exit CLI mode

# 🔲 Create the GUI window (Optional)
root = tk.Tk()
root.title("SOC Tool")
root.geometry("400x400")
root.resizable(False, False)

# Header
tk.Label(root, text="Marchex SOC Tool", font=("Arial", 16, "bold")).pack(pady=20)

# Buttons for Access Actions
tk.Button(root, text="Check Access", font=("Arial", 12),
          command=open_check_access_window, width=25, height=2).pack(pady=5)

tk.Button(root, text="Grant Access", font=("Arial", 12),
          command=lambda: open_access_window("Grant", GRANT_ACCESS_SCRIPT), width=25, height=2).pack(pady=5)

tk.Button(root, text="Remove Access", font=("Arial", 12),
          command=lambda: open_access_window("Remove", SEPARATIONS_SCRIPT), width=25, height=2).pack(pady=5)

tk.Button(root, text="Clear RT Queue", font=("Arial", 12),
          command=lambda: subprocess.run(["python", CLEAR_RT_SCRIPT]), width=25, height=2).pack(pady=5)

# ✅ Start GUI event loop
root.mainloop()

"""  
SOC Access Management Tool (GUI Optional) ----------------------------------------- This script provides a simple interface for SOC access management: - Check Access - Grant Access - Remove Access - Clear RT Queue  🛠️ Designed for both CLI and GUI operation. ✅ Follows Matt's guidelines: maintainability, simplicity, and clarity. """  import sys import os  # Dynamically add the Utils directory to sys.path (works regardless of where the script is executed) BASE_DIR = os.path.dirname(os.path.abspath(__file__))  # Get the directory of soctool.py UTILS_DIR = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "Utils")  # Locate the Utils folder sys.path.append(UTILS_DIR)  # Add Utils to Python path to import shared utilities  # Importing necessary modules from rt_api import add_comment  # Import function for RT API ticket updates  import tkinter as tk  # GUI module for user interface from tkinter import messagebox  # For popup error messages in GUI import subprocess  # Allows running external Python scripts import threading  # Used for running scripts without freezing the GUI  # Import Check Access function from its respective module from CheckAccess.checkaccess import open_check_access_window    # ✅ Define paths to access management scripts GRANT_ACCESS_SCRIPT = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "GrantAccess", "grantaccess.py")  # Grant access script SEPARATIONS_SCRIPT = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "RemoveAccess", "separation.py")  # Remove access script CLEAR_RT_SCRIPT = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "close_cleared_rts.py")  # Clear RT queue script   def open_access_window(action, script_path):     """     Opens a GUI window for granting or removing access.     Allows the SOC user to input their LDAP credentials, the target user, and an optional RT ticket number.      Args:         action (str): "Grant" or "Remove" (determines window title and action).         script_path (str): Path to the corresponding access management script.     """      # Create a new pop-up window for user input     action_window = tk.Toplevel(root)     action_window.title(f"SOC - {action} Access")  # Window title     action_window.geometry("500x525")  # Set window size      # Header Label     tk.Label(action_window, text=f"{action} User Access", font=("Arial", 14, "bold")).pack(pady=10)      # LDAP Credentials Input     tk.Label(action_window, text="Enter your LDAP username:").pack()     ldap_entry = tk.Entry(action_window, width=40)     ldap_entry.pack(pady=5)      tk.Label(action_window, text="Enter your LDAP password:").pack()     ldap_pass_entry = tk.Entry(action_window, width=40, show="*")  # Mask password input     ldap_pass_entry.pack(pady=5)      # Target User Input     tk.Label(action_window, text=f"Enter LDAP username to {action.lower()} access for:").pack()     target_user_entry = tk.Entry(action_window, width=40)     target_user_entry.pack(pady=5)      # RT Ticket Number (Optional)     tk.Label(action_window, text="Enter RT Ticket Number (Optional):").pack()     rt_ticket_entry = tk.Entry(action_window, width=40)     rt_ticket_entry.pack(pady=5)      # Mock Mode Toggle (enabled by default)     mock_mode = tk.BooleanVar(value=True)  # Default is ON     tk.Checkbutton(action_window, text="Enable Mock Mode", variable=mock_mode).pack()      # Log display area for script output     tk.Label(action_window, text="Logs:").pack()     log_area = tk.Text(action_window, width=60, height=10)     log_area.pack(pady=5)      def execute_action():         """         Executes the selected access action (Grant or Remove) with user input values.         Runs in a separate thread to keep the GUI responsive.         """         ldap_user = ldap_entry.get().strip()  # Get LDAP username         ldap_pass = ldap_pass_entry.get().strip()  # Get LDAP password         target_user = target_user_entry.get().strip()  # Get target username         rt_ticket = rt_ticket_entry.get().strip()  # Get RT ticket number (if provided)         mock_flag = "--mock" if mock_mode.get() else ""  # Determine if mock mode is enabled          # Ensure required fields are filled         if not ldap_user or not ldap_pass or not target_user:             messagebox.showerror("Error", "All fields are required except RT Ticket.")  # Show error popup             return          log_area.insert(tk.END, f"🚀 Running {action} script for {target_user}...\n")         log_area.see(tk.END)          def execute():             """             Calls the corresponding access management script with user input.             Captures and displays script output in the log area.             """             try:                 result = subprocess.run(                     ["python", script_path, ldap_user, ldap_pass, target_user, rt_ticket, mock_flag],                     capture_output=True, text=True                 )                 log_area.insert(tk.END, result.stdout + "\n")  # Log script output                 log_area.insert(tk.END, result.stderr + "\n")  # Log any errors             except subprocess.CalledProcessError as e:                 log_area.insert(tk.END, f"❌ Error: {e.stderr}\n")  # Log execution error          # Run the script execution in a separate thread to prevent UI freezing         threading.Thread(target=execute, daemon=True).start()      # Execute Button     tk.Button(action_window, text="Execute", command=execute_action, font=("Arial", 12), width=20).pack(pady=10)   # ✅ Start GUI event loop root.mainloop()     since the soctool script has the open_access_window function it not nessisary to have the open_check_access_window, open_grant_access_window, and  open_remove_access_window in the other 3 scripts right?     """ SOC Access Check Script ----------------------------------------- Checks a user's access across multiple SOC systems.  🛠️ Features: - Runs system-specific access checks via external scripts. - Logs results in Logs/SOC_Access_Log.txt. - Automatically updates an RT ticket (if provided). ✅ Designed for both CLI and GUI operation. """  import threading import argparse import logging import os import subprocess import sys import tkinter as tk from tkinter import messagebox, scrolledtext from datetime import datetime  # Ensure Utils is accessible for rt_api.py BASE_DIR = os.path.dirname(os.path.abspath(__file__))  # Get current script location UTILS_DIR = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "..", "Utils")  # Locate Utils folder sys.path.append(UTILS_DIR)  # Add to system path  from rt_api import add_comment  # Import RT API functionality  # ✅ Define directory for system-specific check scripts SYSTEMS_DIR = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "Systems")  # ✅ Ensure logs are stored in a Logs folder LOG_DIR = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "..", "Logs") os.makedirs(LOG_DIR, exist_ok=True)  # Create Logs directory if missing LOG_FILE = os.path.join(LOG_DIR, "SOC_Access_Log.txt")  logging.basicConfig(filename=LOG_FILE, format='%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s', level=logging.INFO)  def check_access(username, ldap_user, ldap_pass, rt_ticket=None, log_area=None):     """     Checks a user's access across multiple SOC systems.      Args:         username (str): The LDAP username to check.         ldap_user (str): The SOC user's LDAP username.         ldap_pass (str): The SOC user's LDAP password.         rt_ticket (str, optional): RT ticket number to log results.         log_area (tk.Text, optional): If provided, logs will be displayed in GUI.     """          timestamp = datetime.now().strftime("%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S")     logging.info(f"===== START: {timestamp} - Checking Access for {username} =====")          results = []      for script in os.listdir(SYSTEMS_DIR):         if script.startswith("check_") and script.endswith(".py"):             system_name = script.replace("check_", "").replace(".py", "").capitalize()             script_path = os.path.join(SYSTEMS_DIR, script)              try:                 result = subprocess.run(                     ["python", script_path, username],                     capture_output=True,                     text=True                 )                 results.append(f"✅ {system_name}: {result.stdout.strip()}")                 logging.info(f"{system_name} - {result.stdout.strip()}")             except Exception as e:                 results.append(f"❌ {system_name}: Error running script - {e}")                 logging.error(f"Error running {system_name} script: {e}")      summary = f"\n🔹 Access check for {username} at {timestamp}\n" + "\n".join(results)      # ✅ Log to RT ticket if provided     if rt_ticket:         add_comment(rt_ticket, summary)      logging.info(f"===== END: {timestamp} - Check Completed for {username} =====\n")      # ✅ If using GUI, update log area     if log_area:         log_area.insert(tk.END, summary + "\n")         log_area.see(tk.END)     else:         print(summary)   def open_check_access_window():     """     Opens a GUI window to check user access.     """      check_window = tk.Toplevel()     check_window.title("Check User Access")     check_window.geometry("500x500")     check_window.minsize(500, 500)  # Ensures the window has a fixed minimum size      tk.Label(check_window, text="Check User Access", font=("Arial", 14, "bold")).pack(pady=10)      # LDAP Credentials     tk.Label(check_window, text="Enter your LDAP username:").pack()     ldap_entry = tk.Entry(check_window, width=40)     ldap_entry.pack(pady=5)      tk.Label(check_window, text="Enter your LDAP password:").pack()     ldap_pass_entry = tk.Entry(check_window, width=40, show="*")     ldap_pass_entry.pack(pady=5)      # Target User     tk.Label(check_window, text="Enter LDAP username to check:").pack()     user_entry = tk.Entry(check_window, width=40)     user_entry.pack(pady=5)      # RT Ticket Number (Optional)     tk.Label(check_window, text="Enter RT Ticket Number (Optional):").pack()     rt_ticket_entry = tk.Entry(check_window, width=40)     rt_ticket_entry.pack(pady=5)      # Log Display     tk.Label(check_window, text="Logs:").pack()     log_area = scrolledtext.ScrolledText(check_window, width=60, height=10)     log_area.pack(pady=5)      def execute_check():         """         Executes the access check and updates the GUI log.         """         ldap_user = ldap_entry.get().strip()         ldap_pass = ldap_pass_entry.get().strip()         check_user = user_entry.get().strip()         rt_ticket = rt_ticket_entry.get().strip()          if not ldap_user or not ldap_pass or not check_user:             messagebox.showerror("Error", "All fields are required except RT Ticket.")             return          log_area.insert(tk.END, f"🚀 Checking access for {check_user}...\n")         log_area.see(tk.END)          threading.Thread(             target=lambda: check_access(check_user, ldap_user, ldap_pass, rt_ticket, log_area),             daemon=True         ).start()      # Execute Button     tk.Button(check_window, text="Execute", command=execute_check, font=("Arial", 12), width=20).pack(pady=10)      # Bind Enter key     check_window.bind('<Return>', lambda event: execute_check())   if __name__ == "__main__":     # ✅ CLI Mode     parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(description="Check user access across SOC systems.")     parser.add_argument("ldap_user", help="Your LDAP username")     parser.add_argument("ldap_pass", help="Your LDAP password")     parser.add_argument("username", help="LDAP username of the user to check")     parser.add_argument("--rt_ticket", help="RT Ticket number for documentation", default=None)      args = parser.parse_args()     check_access(args.username, args.ldap_user, args.ldap_pass, args.rt_ticket)     """ SOC Access Granting Script (GUI Supported) ----------------------------------------- Grants access to a user across multiple SOC systems.  🛠️ Features: - Runs system-specific grant scripts - Logs results in Logs/SOC_Access_Log.txt - Provides GUI for input or can run via CLI - Automatically updates an RT ticket (if provided) """  import threading import argparse import logging import os import subprocess import sys import tkinter as tk from tkinter import messagebox, scrolledtext from datetime import datetime  # Ensure Utils is accessible for rt_api.py BASE_DIR = os.path.dirname(os.path.abspath(__file__)) UTILS_DIR = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "..", "Utils") sys.path.append(UTILS_DIR)  from rt_api import add_comment  # Import RT API functionality  # ✅ Define path to system grant scripts inside GrantAccess/Systems/ SYSTEMS_DIR = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "Systems")  # ✅ Ensure logs are stored in a Logs folder LOG_DIR = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "..", "Logs") os.makedirs(LOG_DIR, exist_ok=True)   LOG_FILE = os.path.join(LOG_DIR, "SOC_Access_Log.txt")  logging.basicConfig(filename=LOG_FILE, format='%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s', level=logging.INFO)  def grant_access(username, ldap_user, ldap_pass, mock_mode=False, rt_ticket=None, log_area=None):     """     Grants access to a user across multiple SOC systems.      Args:         username (str): The LDAP username to grant access to.         ldap_user (str): The SOC user's LDAP username.         ldap_pass (str): The SOC user's LDAP password.         mock_mode (bool): Whether to run in mock mode (no real changes).         rt_ticket (str, optional): RT ticket number for logging the access grant.         log_area (tk.Text, optional): GUI log display area.     """          timestamp = datetime.now().strftime("%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S")     logging.info(f"===== START: {timestamp} - Granting Access for {username} =====")          results = []      for script in os.listdir(SYSTEMS_DIR):         if script.startswith("grant_") and script.endswith(".py"):             system = script.replace("grant_", "").replace(".py", "").capitalize()             script_path = os.path.join(SYSTEMS_DIR, script)              try:                 cmd = ["python", script_path, username, "grant"]                 if mock_mode:                     cmd.append("--mock")                  result = subprocess.run(cmd, capture_output=True, text=True)                 results.append(f"✅ {system}: {result.stdout.strip()}")                 logging.info(f"{system} - {result.stdout.strip()}")             except Exception as e:                 results.append(f"❌ {system}: Error running script - {e}")                 logging.error(f"Error running {system} script: {e}")      summary = f"\n🔹 Access granted for {username} at {timestamp}\n" + "\n".join(results)      # ✅ Log to RT ticket if provided     if rt_ticket:         add_comment(rt_ticket, summary)      logging.info(f"===== END: {timestamp} - Granting Complete for {username} =====\n")      if log_area:         log_area.insert(tk.END, summary + "\n")         log_area.see(tk.END)     else:         print(summary)   def open_grant_access_window():     """     Opens a GUI window for granting user access.     """      grant_window = tk.Toplevel()     grant_window.title("Grant User Access")     grant_window.geometry("500x725")     #grant_window.minsize(500, 525)  # Ensures the window has a fixed minimum size       tk.Label(grant_window, text="Grant User Access", font=("Arial", 14, "bold")).pack(pady=10)      # LDAP Credentials     tk.Label(grant_window, text="Enter your LDAP username:").pack()     ldap_entry = tk.Entry(grant_window, width=40)     ldap_entry.pack(pady=5)      tk.Label(grant_window, text="Enter your LDAP password:").pack()     ldap_pass_entry = tk.Entry(grant_window, width=40, show="*")     ldap_pass_entry.pack(pady=5)      # Target User     tk.Label(grant_window, text="Enter LDAP username to grant access to:").pack()     user_entry = tk.Entry(grant_window, width=40)     user_entry.pack(pady=5)      # RT Ticket Number (Optional)     tk.Label(grant_window, text="Enter RT Ticket Number (Optional):").pack()     rt_ticket_entry = tk.Entry(grant_window, width=40)     rt_ticket_entry.pack(pady=5)      # Mock Mode Toggle     mock_mode = tk.BooleanVar(value=True)     tk.Checkbutton(grant_window, text="Enable Mock Mode", variable=mock_mode).pack()      # Log Display     tk.Label(grant_window, text="Logs:").pack()     log_area = scrolledtext.ScrolledText(grant_window, width=60, height=10)     log_area.pack(pady=5)      def execute_grant():         """         Executes the grant access script and updates the GUI log.         """         ldap_user = ldap_entry.get().strip()         ldap_pass = ldap_pass_entry.get().strip()         grant_user = user_entry.get().strip()         rt_ticket = rt_ticket_entry.get().strip()          if not ldap_user or not ldap_pass or not grant_user:             messagebox.showerror("Error", "All fields are required except RT Ticket.")             return          log_area.insert(tk.END, f"🚀 Granting access for {grant_user}...\n")         log_area.see(tk.END)          threading.Thread(             target=lambda: grant_access(grant_user, ldap_user, ldap_pass, mock_mode.get(), rt_ticket, log_area),             daemon=True         ).start()      tk.Button(grant_window, text="Execute", command=execute_grant, font=("Arial", 12), width=20).pack(pady=10)      grant_window.bind('<Return>', lambda event: execute_grant())  # ✅ Add CLI mode for direct execution if __name__ == "__main__":     parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(description="Grant user access to SOC systems.")     parser.add_argument("ldap_user", help="Your LDAP username")     parser.add_argument("ldap_pass", help="Your LDAP password")     parser.add_argument("username", help="LDAP username of the user to grant access")     parser.add_argument("--mock", action="store_true", help="Enable mock mode (no real changes)")     parser.add_argument("--rt_ticket", help="RT Ticket number for documentation", default=None)      args = parser.parse_args()     grant_access(args.username, args.ldap_user, args.ldap_pass, args.mock, args.rt_ticket)     """ SOC Access Removal Script (GUI Supported) ----------------------------------------- Removes access from a user across multiple SOC systems.  🛠️ Features: - Runs system-specific removal scripts. - Logs results in Logs/SOC_Access_Log.txt. - Provides GUI for input or can run via CLI. - Automatically updates an RT ticket (if provided). """  import threading import argparse import logging import os import subprocess import sys import tkinter as tk from tkinter import messagebox, scrolledtext from datetime import datetime  # Ensure Utils is accessible for rt_api.py BASE_DIR = os.path.dirname(os.path.abspath(__file__)) UTILS_DIR = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "..", "Utils") sys.path.append(UTILS_DIR)  from rt_api import add_comment  # Import RT API functionality  # ✅ Define path to system removal scripts inside RemoveAccess/Systems/ SYSTEMS_DIR = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "Systems")  # ✅ Ensure logs are stored in a Logs folder LOG_DIR = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "..", "Logs") os.makedirs(LOG_DIR, exist_ok=True)  # Create Logs directory if missing LOG_FILE = os.path.join(LOG_DIR, "SOC_Access_Log.txt")  logging.basicConfig(filename=LOG_FILE, format='%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s', level=logging.INFO)  def remove_access(username, ldap_user, ldap_pass, mock_mode=False, rt_ticket=None, log_area=None):     """     Removes access for a user across multiple SOC systems.      Args:         username (str): The LDAP username whose access is being removed.         ldap_user (str): The SOC user's LDAP username.         ldap_pass (str): The SOC user's LDAP password.         mock_mode (bool): Whether to run in mock mode (no real changes).         rt_ticket (str, optional): RT ticket number to log results.         log_area (tk.Text, optional): GUI log display area.     """      timestamp = datetime.now().strftime("%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S")     logging.info(f"===== START: {timestamp} - Removing Access for {username} =====")          results = []      for script in os.listdir(SYSTEMS_DIR):         if script.startswith("remove_") and script.endswith(".py"):             system = script.replace("remove_", "").replace(".py", "").capitalize()             script_path = os.path.join(SYSTEMS_DIR, script)              try:                 cmd = ["python", script_path, username, "remove"]                 if mock_mode:                     cmd.append("--mock")                  result = subprocess.run(cmd, capture_output=True, text=True)                 results.append(f"✅ {system}: {result.stdout.strip()}")                 logging.info(f"{system} - {result.stdout.strip()}")             except Exception as e:                 results.append(f"❌ {system}: Error running script - {e}")                 logging.error(f"Error running {system} script: {e}")      summary = f"\n🔹 Removal completed for {username} at {timestamp}\n" + "\n".join(results)      # ✅ Log to RT ticket if provided     if rt_ticket:         add_comment(rt_ticket, summary)      logging.info(f"===== END: {timestamp} - Removal Complete for {username} =====\n")      if log_area:         log_area.insert(tk.END, summary + "\n")         log_area.see(tk.END)     else:         print(summary)   def open_remove_access_window():     """     Opens a GUI window for removing user access.     """      remove_window = tk.Toplevel()     remove_window.title("Remove User Access")     remove_window.geometry("500x525")     remove_window.minsize(500, 525)  # Ensures the window has a fixed minimum size      tk.Label(remove_window, text="Remove User Access", font=("Arial", 14, "bold")).pack(pady=10)      # LDAP Credentials     tk.Label(remove_window, text="Enter your LDAP username:").pack()     ldap_entry = tk.Entry(remove_window, width=40)     ldap_entry.pack(pady=5)      tk.Label(remove_window, text="Enter your LDAP password:").pack()     ldap_pass_entry = tk.Entry(remove_window, width=40, show="*")     ldap_pass_entry.pack(pady=5)      # Target User     tk.Label(remove_window, text="Enter LDAP username to remove access from:").pack()     user_entry = tk.Entry(remove_window, width=40)     user_entry.pack(pady=5)      # RT Ticket Number (Optional)     tk.Label(remove_window, text="Enter RT Ticket Number (Optional):").pack()     rt_ticket_entry = tk.Entry(remove_window, width=40)     rt_ticket_entry.pack(pady=5)      # Mock Mode Toggle     mock_mode = tk.BooleanVar(value=True)     tk.Checkbutton(remove_window, text="Enable Mock Mode", variable=mock_mode).pack()      # Log Display     tk.Label(remove_window, text="Logs:").pack()     log_area = scrolledtext.ScrolledText(remove_window, width=60, height=10)     log_area.pack(pady=5)      def execute_remove():         """         Executes the remove access script and updates the GUI log.         """         ldap_user = ldap_entry.get().strip()         ldap_pass = ldap_pass_entry.get().strip()         remove_user = user_entry.get().strip()         rt_ticket = rt_ticket_entry.get().strip()          if not ldap_user or not ldap_pass or not remove_user:             messagebox.showerror("Error", "All fields are required except RT Ticket.")             return          log_area.insert(tk.END, f"🚀 Removing access for {remove_user}...\n")         log_area.see(tk.END)          threading.Thread(             target=lambda: remove_access(remove_user, ldap_user, ldap_pass, mock_mode.get(), rt_ticket, log_area),             daemon=True         ).start()      tk.Button(remove_window, text="Execute", command=execute_remove, font=("Arial", 12), width=20).pack(pady=10)      remove_window.bind('<Return>', lambda event: execute_remove())  # ✅ Add CLI mode for direct execution if __name__ == "__main__":     parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(description="Remove user access from SOC systems.")     parser.add_argument("ldap_user", help="Your LDAP username")     parser.add_argument("ldap_pass", help="Your LDAP password")     parser.add_argument("username", help="LDAP username of the user to remove access from")     parser.add_argument("--mock", action="store_true", help="Enable mock mode (no real changes)")     parser.add_argument("--rt_ticket", help="RT Ticket number for documentation", default=None)      args = parser.parse_args()     remove_access(args.username, args.ldap_user, args.ldap_pass, args.mock, args.rt_ticket) 
"""
SOC Access Management Tool (GUI Optional)
-----------------------------------------
This script provides a simple interface for SOC access management:
- Check Access
- Grant Access
- Remove Access
- Clear RT Queue

🛠️ Designed for both CLI and GUI operation.
✅ Follows Matt's guidelines: maintainability, simplicity, and clarity.
"""

import sys
import os

# Dynamically add the Utils directory to sys.path (works regardless of where the script is executed)
BASE_DIR = os.path.dirname(os.path.abspath(__file__))  # Get the directory of soctool.py
UTILS_DIR = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "Utils")  # Locate the Utils folder
sys.path.append(UTILS_DIR)  # Add Utils to Python path to import shared utilities

# Importing necessary modules
from rt_api import add_comment  # Import function for RT API ticket updates

import tkinter as tk  # GUI module for user interface
from tkinter import messagebox  # For popup error messages in GUI
import subprocess  # Allows running external Python scripts
import threading  # Used for running scripts without freezing the GUI

# Import Check Access function from its respective module
from CheckAccess.checkaccess import open_check_access_window  

# ✅ Define paths to access management scripts
GRANT_ACCESS_SCRIPT = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "GrantAccess", "grantaccess.py")  # Grant access script
SEPARATIONS_SCRIPT = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "RemoveAccess", "separation.py")  # Remove access script
CLEAR_RT_SCRIPT = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "close_cleared_rts.py")  # Clear RT queue script


def open_access_window(action, script_path):
    """
    Opens a GUI window for granting or removing access.
    Allows the SOC user to input their LDAP credentials, the target user, and an optional RT ticket number.

    Args:
        action (str): "Grant" or "Remove" (determines window title and action).
        script_path (str): Path to the corresponding access management script.
    """

    # Create a new pop-up window for user input
    action_window = tk.Toplevel(root)
    action_window.title(f"SOC - {action} Access")  # Window title
    action_window.geometry("500x525")  # Set window size

    # Header Label
    tk.Label(action_window, text=f"{action} User Access", font=("Arial", 14, "bold")).pack(pady=10)

    # LDAP Credentials Input
    tk.Label(action_window, text="Enter your LDAP username:").pack()
    ldap_entry = tk.Entry(action_window, width=40)
    ldap_entry.pack(pady=5)

    tk.Label(action_window, text="Enter your LDAP password:").pack()
    ldap_pass_entry = tk.Entry(action_window, width=40, show="*")  # Mask password input
    ldap_pass_entry.pack(pady=5)

    # Target User Input
    tk.Label(action_window, text=f"Enter LDAP username to {action.lower()} access for:").pack()
    target_user_entry = tk.Entry(action_window, width=40)
    target_user_entry.pack(pady=5)

    # RT Ticket Number (Optional)
    tk.Label(action_window, text="Enter RT Ticket Number (Optional):").pack()
    rt_ticket_entry = tk.Entry(action_window, width=40)
    rt_ticket_entry.pack(pady=5)

    # Mock Mode Toggle (enabled by default)
    mock_mode = tk.BooleanVar(value=True)  # Default is ON
    tk.Checkbutton(action_window, text="Enable Mock Mode", variable=mock_mode).pack()

    # Log display area for script output
    tk.Label(action_window, text="Logs:").pack()
    log_area = tk.Text(action_window, width=60, height=10)
    log_area.pack(pady=5)

    def execute_action():
        """
        Executes the selected access action (Grant or Remove) with user input values.
        Runs in a separate thread to keep the GUI responsive.
        """
        ldap_user = ldap_entry.get().strip()  # Get LDAP username
        ldap_pass = ldap_pass_entry.get().strip()  # Get LDAP password
        target_user = target_user_entry.get().strip()  # Get target username
        rt_ticket = rt_ticket_entry.get().strip()  # Get RT ticket number (if provided)
        mock_flag = "--mock" if mock_mode.get() else ""  # Determine if mock mode is enabled

        # Ensure required fields are filled
        if not ldap_user or not ldap_pass or not target_user:
            messagebox.showerror("Error", "All fields are required except RT Ticket.")  # Show error popup
            return

        log_area.insert(tk.END, f"🚀 Running {action} script for {target_user}...\n")
        log_area.see(tk.END)

        def execute():
            """
            Calls the corresponding access management script with user input.
            Captures and displays script output in the log area.
            """
            try:
                result = subprocess.run(
                    ["python", script_path, ldap_user, ldap_pass, target_user, rt_ticket, mock_flag],
                    capture_output=True, text=True
                )
                log_area.insert(tk.END, result.stdout + "\n")  # Log script output
                log_area.insert(tk.END, result.stderr + "\n")  # Log any errors
            except subprocess.CalledProcessError as e:
                log_area.insert(tk.END, f"❌ Error: {e.stderr}\n")  # Log execution error

        # Run the script execution in a separate thread to prevent UI freezing
        threading.Thread(target=execute, daemon=True).start()

    # Execute Button
    tk.Button(action_window, text="Execute", command=execute_action, font=("Arial", 12), width=20).pack(pady=10)


# ✅ CLI Mode: If run with arguments, show usage instructions
if len(sys.argv) > 1:
    print("\nSOC Access Management Tool (GUI Optional)")
    print("==========================================")
    print("Usage:")
    print("  python soctool.py   # Starts GUI")
    print("  Run individual scripts (separation.py, grantaccess.py) for CLI access")
    sys.exit()  # Exit CLI mode to prevent GUI from launching

# 🔲 Create the GUI window (Optional)
root = tk.Tk()
root.title("SOC Tool")  # Set window title
root.geometry("400x400")  # Set window size
root.resizable(False, False)  # Disable resizing

# Header Label
tk.Label(root, text="Marchex SOC Tool", font=("Arial", 16, "bold")).pack(pady=20)

# Buttons for Access Actions
tk.Button(root, text="Check Access", font=("Arial", 12),
          command=open_check_access_window, width=25, height=2).pack(pady=5)

tk.Button(root, text="Grant Access", font=("Arial", 12),
          command=lambda: open_access_window("Grant", GRANT_ACCESS_SCRIPT), width=25, height=2).pack(pady=5)

tk.Button(root, text="Remove Access", font=("Arial", 12),
          command=lambda: open_access_window("Remove", SEPARATIONS_SCRIPT), width=25, height=2).pack(pady=5)

tk.Button(root, text="Clear RT Queue", font=("Arial", 12),
          command=lambda: subprocess.run(["python", CLEAR_RT_SCRIPT]), width=25, height=2).pack(pady=5)

# ✅ Start GUI event loop
root.mainloop()




"""
SOC Access Check Script
-----------------------------------------
Checks a user's access across multiple SOC systems.

🛠️ Features:
- Runs system-specific access checks via external scripts.
- Logs results in Logs/SOC_Access_Log.txt.
- Automatically updates an RT ticket (if provided).
✅ Designed for both CLI and GUI operation.
"""

import threading
import argparse
import logging
import os
import subprocess
import sys
import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import messagebox, scrolledtext
from datetime import datetime

# Ensure Utils is accessible for rt_api.py
BASE_DIR = os.path.dirname(os.path.abspath(__file__))  # Get current script location
UTILS_DIR = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "..", "Utils")  # Locate Utils folder
sys.path.append(UTILS_DIR)  # Add to system path

from rt_api import add_comment  # Import RT API functionality

# ✅ Define directory for system-specific check scripts
SYSTEMS_DIR = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "Systems")

# ✅ Ensure logs are stored in a Logs folder
LOG_DIR = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "..", "Logs")
os.makedirs(LOG_DIR, exist_ok=True)  # Create Logs directory if missing
LOG_FILE = os.path.join(LOG_DIR, "SOC_Access_Log.txt")

logging.basicConfig(filename=LOG_FILE, format='%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s', level=logging.INFO)

def check_access(username, ldap_user, ldap_pass, rt_ticket=None, log_area=None):
    """
    Checks a user's access across multiple SOC systems.

    Args:
        username (str): The LDAP username to check.
        ldap_user (str): The SOC user's LDAP username.
        ldap_pass (str): The SOC user's LDAP password.
        rt_ticket (str, optional): RT ticket number to log results.
        log_area (tk.Text, optional): If provided, logs will be displayed in GUI.
    """
    
    timestamp = datetime.now().strftime("%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S")
    logging.info(f"===== START: {timestamp} - Checking Access for {username} =====")
    
    results = []

    for script in os.listdir(SYSTEMS_DIR):
        if script.startswith("check_") and script.endswith(".py"):
            system_name = script.replace("check_", "").replace(".py", "").capitalize()
            script_path = os.path.join(SYSTEMS_DIR, script)

            try:
                result = subprocess.run(
                    ["python", script_path, username],
                    capture_output=True,
                    text=True
                )
                results.append(f"✅ {system_name}: {result.stdout.strip()}")
                logging.info(f"{system_name} - {result.stdout.strip()}")
            except Exception as e:
                results.append(f"❌ {system_name}: Error running script - {e}")
                logging.error(f"Error running {system_name} script: {e}")

    summary = f"\n🔹 Access check for {username} at {timestamp}\n" + "\n".join(results)

    # ✅ Log to RT ticket if provided
    if rt_ticket:
        add_comment(rt_ticket, summary)

    logging.info(f"===== END: {timestamp} - Check Completed for {username} =====\n")

    # ✅ If using GUI, update log area
    if log_area:
        log_area.insert(tk.END, summary + "\n")
        log_area.see(tk.END)
    else:
        print(summary)


def open_check_access_window():
    """
    Opens a GUI window to check user access.
    """

    check_window = tk.Toplevel()
    check_window.title("Check User Access")
    check_window.geometry("500x500")
    check_window.minsize(500, 500)  # Ensures the window has a fixed minimum size

    tk.Label(check_window, text="Check User Access", font=("Arial", 14, "bold")).pack(pady=10)

    # LDAP Credentials
    tk.Label(check_window, text="Enter your LDAP username:").pack()
    ldap_entry = tk.Entry(check_window, width=40)
    ldap_entry.pack(pady=5)

    tk.Label(check_window, text="Enter your LDAP password:").pack()
    ldap_pass_entry = tk.Entry(check_window, width=40, show="*")
    ldap_pass_entry.pack(pady=5)

    # Target User
    tk.Label(check_window, text="Enter LDAP username to check:").pack()
    user_entry = tk.Entry(check_window, width=40)
    user_entry.pack(pady=5)

    # RT Ticket Number (Optional)
    tk.Label(check_window, text="Enter RT Ticket Number (Optional):").pack()
    rt_ticket_entry = tk.Entry(check_window, width=40)
    rt_ticket_entry.pack(pady=5)

    # Log Display
    tk.Label(check_window, text="Logs:").pack()
    log_area = scrolledtext.ScrolledText(check_window, width=60, height=10)
    log_area.pack(pady=5)

    def execute_check():
        """
        Executes the access check and updates the GUI log.
        """
        ldap_user = ldap_entry.get().strip()
        ldap_pass = ldap_pass_entry.get().strip()
        check_user = user_entry.get().strip()
        rt_ticket = rt_ticket_entry.get().strip()

        if not ldap_user or not ldap_pass or not check_user:
            messagebox.showerror("Error", "All fields are required except RT Ticket.")
            return

        log_area.insert(tk.END, f"🚀 Checking access for {check_user}...\n")
        log_area.see(tk.END)

        threading.Thread(
            target=lambda: check_access(check_user, ldap_user, ldap_pass, rt_ticket, log_area),
            daemon=True
        ).start()

    # Execute Button
    tk.Button(check_window, text="Execute", command=execute_check, font=("Arial", 12), width=20).pack(pady=10)

    # Bind Enter key
    check_window.bind('<Return>', lambda event: execute_check())


if __name__ == "__main__":
    # ✅ CLI Mode
    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(description="Check user access across SOC systems.")
    parser.add_argument("ldap_user", help="Your LDAP username")
    parser.add_argument("ldap_pass", help="Your LDAP password")
    parser.add_argument("username", help="LDAP username of the user to check")
    parser.add_argument("--rt_ticket", help="RT Ticket number for documentation", default=None)

    args = parser.parse_args()
    check_access(args.username, args.ldap_user, args.ldap_pass, args.rt_ticket)




"""
SOC Access Granting Script (GUI Supported)
-----------------------------------------
Grants access to a user across multiple SOC systems.

🛠️ Features:
- Runs system-specific grant scripts
- Logs results in Logs/SOC_Access_Log.txt
- Provides GUI for input or can run via CLI
- Automatically updates an RT ticket (if provided)
"""

import threading
import argparse
import logging
import os
import subprocess
import sys
import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import messagebox, scrolledtext
from datetime import datetime

# Ensure Utils is accessible for rt_api.py
BASE_DIR = os.path.dirname(os.path.abspath(__file__))
UTILS_DIR = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "..", "Utils")
sys.path.append(UTILS_DIR)

from rt_api import add_comment  # Import RT API functionality

# ✅ Define path to system grant scripts inside GrantAccess/Systems/
SYSTEMS_DIR = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "Systems")

# ✅ Ensure logs are stored in a Logs folder
LOG_DIR = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "..", "Logs")
os.makedirs(LOG_DIR, exist_ok=True)  
LOG_FILE = os.path.join(LOG_DIR, "SOC_Access_Log.txt")

logging.basicConfig(filename=LOG_FILE, format='%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s', level=logging.INFO)

def grant_access(username, ldap_user, ldap_pass, mock_mode=False, rt_ticket=None, log_area=None):
    """
    Grants access to a user across multiple SOC systems.

    Args:
        username (str): The LDAP username to grant access to.
        ldap_user (str): The SOC user's LDAP username.
        ldap_pass (str): The SOC user's LDAP password.
        mock_mode (bool): Whether to run in mock mode (no real changes).
        rt_ticket (str, optional): RT ticket number for logging the access grant.
        log_area (tk.Text, optional): GUI log display area.
    """
    
    timestamp = datetime.now().strftime("%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S")
    logging.info(f"===== START: {timestamp} - Granting Access for {username} =====")
    
    results = []

    for script in os.listdir(SYSTEMS_DIR):
        if script.startswith("grant_") and script.endswith(".py"):
            system = script.replace("grant_", "").replace(".py", "").capitalize()
            script_path = os.path.join(SYSTEMS_DIR, script)

            try:
                cmd = ["python", script_path, username, "grant"]
                if mock_mode:
                    cmd.append("--mock")

                result = subprocess.run(cmd, capture_output=True, text=True)
                results.append(f"✅ {system}: {result.stdout.strip()}")
                logging.info(f"{system} - {result.stdout.strip()}")
            except Exception as e:
                results.append(f"❌ {system}: Error running script - {e}")
                logging.error(f"Error running {system} script: {e}")

    summary = f"\n🔹 Access granted for {username} at {timestamp}\n" + "\n".join(results)

    # ✅ Log to RT ticket if provided
    if rt_ticket:
        add_comment(rt_ticket, summary)

    logging.info(f"===== END: {timestamp} - Granting Complete for {username} =====\n")

    if log_area:
        log_area.insert(tk.END, summary + "\n")
        log_area.see(tk.END)
    else:
        print(summary)


def open_grant_access_window():
    """
    Opens a GUI window for granting user access.
    """

    grant_window = tk.Toplevel()
    grant_window.title("Grant User Access")
    grant_window.geometry("500x725")
    #grant_window.minsize(500, 525)  # Ensures the window has a fixed minimum size


    tk.Label(grant_window, text="Grant User Access", font=("Arial", 14, "bold")).pack(pady=10)

    # LDAP Credentials
    tk.Label(grant_window, text="Enter your LDAP username:").pack()
    ldap_entry = tk.Entry(grant_window, width=40)
    ldap_entry.pack(pady=5)

    tk.Label(grant_window, text="Enter your LDAP password:").pack()
    ldap_pass_entry = tk.Entry(grant_window, width=40, show="*")
    ldap_pass_entry.pack(pady=5)

    # Target User
    tk.Label(grant_window, text="Enter LDAP username to grant access to:").pack()
    user_entry = tk.Entry(grant_window, width=40)
    user_entry.pack(pady=5)

    # RT Ticket Number (Optional)
    tk.Label(grant_window, text="Enter RT Ticket Number (Optional):").pack()
    rt_ticket_entry = tk.Entry(grant_window, width=40)
    rt_ticket_entry.pack(pady=5)

    # Mock Mode Toggle
    mock_mode = tk.BooleanVar(value=True)
    tk.Checkbutton(grant_window, text="Enable Mock Mode", variable=mock_mode).pack()

    # Log Display
    tk.Label(grant_window, text="Logs:").pack()
    log_area = scrolledtext.ScrolledText(grant_window, width=60, height=10)
    log_area.pack(pady=5)

    def execute_grant():
        """
        Executes the grant access script and updates the GUI log.
        """
        ldap_user = ldap_entry.get().strip()
        ldap_pass = ldap_pass_entry.get().strip()
        grant_user = user_entry.get().strip()
        rt_ticket = rt_ticket_entry.get().strip()

        if not ldap_user or not ldap_pass or not grant_user:
            messagebox.showerror("Error", "All fields are required except RT Ticket.")
            return

        log_area.insert(tk.END, f"🚀 Granting access for {grant_user}...\n")
        log_area.see(tk.END)

        threading.Thread(
            target=lambda: grant_access(grant_user, ldap_user, ldap_pass, mock_mode.get(), rt_ticket, log_area),
            daemon=True
        ).start()

    tk.Button(grant_window, text="Execute", command=execute_grant, font=("Arial", 12), width=20).pack(pady=10)

    grant_window.bind('<Return>', lambda event: execute_grant())

# ✅ Add CLI mode for direct execution
if __name__ == "__main__":
    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(description="Grant user access to SOC systems.")
    parser.add_argument("ldap_user", help="Your LDAP username")
    parser.add_argument("ldap_pass", help="Your LDAP password")
    parser.add_argument("username", help="LDAP username of the user to grant access")
    parser.add_argument("--mock", action="store_true", help="Enable mock mode (no real changes)")
    parser.add_argument("--rt_ticket", help="RT Ticket number for documentation", default=None)

    args = parser.parse_args()
    grant_access(args.username, args.ldap_user, args.ldap_pass, args.mock, args.rt_ticket)

"""
SOC Access Check Script
-----------------------------------------
Checks a user's access across multiple SOC systems.

🛠️ Features:
- Runs system-specific access checks via external scripts.
- Logs results in Logs/SOC_Access_Log.txt.
- Automatically updates an RT ticket (if provided).
✅ Designed for both CLI and GUI operation.
"""

import threading
import argparse
import logging
import os
import subprocess
import sys
import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import messagebox, scrolledtext
from datetime import datetime

# Ensure Utils is accessible for rt_api.py
BASE_DIR = os.path.dirname(os.path.abspath(__file__))  # Get current script location
UTILS_DIR = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "..", "Utils")  # Locate Utils folder
sys.path.append(UTILS_DIR)  # Add to system path

from rt_api import add_comment  # Import RT API functionality

# ✅ Define directory for system-specific check scripts
SYSTEMS_DIR = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "Systems")

# ✅ Ensure logs are stored in a Logs folder
LOG_DIR = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "..", "Logs")
os.makedirs(LOG_DIR, exist_ok=True)  # Create Logs directory if missing
LOG_FILE = os.path.join(LOG_DIR, "SOC_Access_Log.txt")

logging.basicConfig(filename=LOG_FILE, format='%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s', level=logging.INFO)

def check_access(username, ldap_user, ldap_pass, rt_ticket=None, log_area=None):
    """
    Checks a user's access across multiple SOC systems.

    Args:
        username (str): The LDAP username to check.
        ldap_user (str): The SOC user's LDAP username.
        ldap_pass (str): The SOC user's LDAP password.
        rt_ticket (str, optional): RT ticket number to log results.
        log_area (tk.Text, optional): If provided, logs will be displayed in GUI.
    """
    
    timestamp = datetime.now().strftime("%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S")
    logging.info(f"===== START: {timestamp} - Checking Access for {username} =====")
    
    results = []

    for script in os.listdir(SYSTEMS_DIR):
        if script.startswith("check_") and script.endswith(".py"):
            system_name = script.replace("check_", "").replace(".py", "").capitalize()
            script_path = os.path.join(SYSTEMS_DIR, script)

            try:
                result = subprocess.run(
                    ["python", script_path, username],
                    capture_output=True,
                    text=True
                )
                results.append(f"✅ {system_name}: {result.stdout.strip()}")
                logging.info(f"{system_name} - {result.stdout.strip()}")
            except Exception as e:
                results.append(f"❌ {system_name}: Error running script - {e}")
                logging.error(f"Error running {system_name} script: {e}")

    summary = f"\n🔹 Access check for {username} at {timestamp}\n" + "\n".join(results)

    # ✅ Log to RT ticket if provided
    if rt_ticket:
        add_comment(rt_ticket, summary)

    logging.info(f"===== END: {timestamp} - Check Completed for {username} =====\n")

    # ✅ If using GUI, update log area
    if log_area:
        log_area.insert(tk.END, summary + "\n")
        log_area.see(tk.END)
    else:
        print(summary)


def open_check_access_window():
    """
    Opens a GUI window to check user access.
    """

    check_window = tk.Toplevel()
    check_window.title("Check User Access")
    check_window.geometry("500x500")
    check_window.minsize(500, 500)  # Ensures the window has a fixed minimum size

    tk.Label(check_window, text="Check User Access", font=("Arial", 14, "bold")).pack(pady=10)

    # LDAP Credentials
    tk.Label(check_window, text="Enter your LDAP username:").pack()
    ldap_entry = tk.Entry(check_window, width=40)
    ldap_entry.pack(pady=5)

    tk.Label(check_window, text="Enter your LDAP password:").pack()
    ldap_pass_entry = tk.Entry(check_window, width=40, show="*")
    ldap_pass_entry.pack(pady=5)

    # Target User
    tk.Label(check_window, text="Enter LDAP username to check:").pack()
    user_entry = tk.Entry(check_window, width=40)
    user_entry.pack(pady=5)

    # RT Ticket Number (Optional)
    tk.Label(check_window, text="Enter RT Ticket Number (Optional):").pack()
    rt_ticket_entry = tk.Entry(check_window, width=40)
    rt_ticket_entry.pack(pady=5)

    # Log Display
    tk.Label(check_window, text="Logs:").pack()
    log_area = scrolledtext.ScrolledText(check_window, width=60, height=10)
    log_area.pack(pady=5)

    def execute_check():
        """
        Executes the access check and updates the GUI log.
        """
        ldap_user = ldap_entry.get().strip()
        ldap_pass = ldap_pass_entry.get().strip()
        check_user = user_entry.get().strip()
        rt_ticket = rt_ticket_entry.get().strip()

        if not ldap_user or not ldap_pass or not check_user:
            messagebox.showerror("Error", "All fields are required except RT Ticket.")
            return

        log_area.insert(tk.END, f"🚀 Checking access for {check_user}...\n")
        log_area.see(tk.END)

        threading.Thread(
            target=lambda: check_access(check_user, ldap_user, ldap_pass, rt_ticket, log_area),
            daemon=True
        ).start()

    # Execute Button
    tk.Button(check_window, text="Execute", command=execute_check, font=("Arial", 12), width=20).pack(pady=10)

    # Bind Enter key
    check_window.bind('<Return>', lambda event: execute_check())


if __name__ == "__main__":
    # ✅ CLI Mode
    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(description="Check user access across SOC systems.")
    parser.add_argument("ldap_user", help="Your LDAP username")
    parser.add_argument("ldap_pass", help="Your LDAP password")
    parser.add_argument("username", help="LDAP username of the user to check")
    parser.add_argument("--rt_ticket", help="RT Ticket number for documentation", default=None)

    args = parser.parse_args()
    check_access(args.username, args.ldap_user, args.ldap_pass, args.rt_ticket)

"""
SOC Access Granting Script (GUI Supported)
-----------------------------------------
Grants access to a user across multiple SOC systems.

🛠️ Features:
- Runs system-specific grant scripts
- Logs results in Logs/SOC_Access_Log.txt
- Provides GUI for input or can run via CLI
- Automatically updates an RT ticket (if provided)
"""

import threading
import argparse
import logging
import os
import subprocess
import sys
import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import messagebox, scrolledtext
from datetime import datetime

# Ensure Utils is accessible for rt_api.py
BASE_DIR = os.path.dirname(os.path.abspath(__file__))
UTILS_DIR = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "..", "Utils")
sys.path.append(UTILS_DIR)

from rt_api import add_comment  # Import RT API functionality

# ✅ Define path to system grant scripts inside GrantAccess/Systems/
SYSTEMS_DIR = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "Systems")

# ✅ Ensure logs are stored in a Logs folder
LOG_DIR = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "..", "Logs")
os.makedirs(LOG_DIR, exist_ok=True)  
LOG_FILE = os.path.join(LOG_DIR, "SOC_Access_Log.txt")

logging.basicConfig(filename=LOG_FILE, format='%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s', level=logging.INFO)

def grant_access(username, ldap_user, ldap_pass, mock_mode=False, rt_ticket=None, log_area=None):
    """
    Grants access to a user across multiple SOC systems.

    Args:
        username (str): The LDAP username to grant access to.
        ldap_user (str): The SOC user's LDAP username.
        ldap_pass (str): The SOC user's LDAP password.
        mock_mode (bool): Whether to run in mock mode (no real changes).
        rt_ticket (str, optional): RT ticket number for logging the access grant.
        log_area (tk.Text, optional): GUI log display area.
    """
    
    timestamp = datetime.now().strftime("%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S")
    logging.info(f"===== START: {timestamp} - Granting Access for {username} =====")
    
    results = []

    for script in os.listdir(SYSTEMS_DIR):
        if script.startswith("grant_") and script.endswith(".py"):
            system = script.replace("grant_", "").replace(".py", "").capitalize()
            script_path = os.path.join(SYSTEMS_DIR, script)

            try:
                cmd = ["python", script_path, username, "grant"]
                if mock_mode:
                    cmd.append("--mock")

                result = subprocess.run(cmd, capture_output=True, text=True)
                results.append(f"✅ {system}: {result.stdout.strip()}")
                logging.info(f"{system} - {result.stdout.strip()}")
            except Exception as e:
                results.append(f"❌ {system}: Error running script - {e}")
                logging.error(f"Error running {system} script: {e}")

    summary = f"\n🔹 Access granted for {username} at {timestamp}\n" + "\n".join(results)

    # ✅ Log to RT ticket if provided
    if rt_ticket:
        add_comment(rt_ticket, summary)

    logging.info(f"===== END: {timestamp} - Granting Complete for {username} =====\n")

    if log_area:
        log_area.insert(tk.END, summary + "\n")
        log_area.see(tk.END)
    else:
        print(summary)

    """
    Opens a GUI window for granting user access.

    grant_window = tk.Toplevel()

    rt_ticket_entry.pack(pady=5)

    # Mock Mode Toggle

        ldap_pass = ldap_pass_entry.get().strip()

    tk.Button(grant_window, text="Execute", command=execute_grant, font=("Arial", 12), width=20).pack(pady=10)

    grant_window.bind('<Return>', lambda event: execute_grant())

"""
SOC RT Ticket Auto-Close Script
-----------------------------------------
This script automatically checks open RT tickets in the SOC Alerts queue
and closes them if the related alert has been cleared.

🛠️ Features:
- Fetches all open RT tickets
- Checks the latest comment for "clear" keywords
- If cleared, resolves & closes the ticket automatically
- Logs all actions in Logs/SOC_RTs_Log.txt
✅ Fully automated with error handling.
"""

import logging
import os
import sys
import rt_marchex as rt  # RT API wrapper

# ✅ Setup Logging in Logs Directory
BASE_DIR = os.path.dirname(os.path.abspath(__file__))  # Get script directory
LOG_DIR = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "Logs")
os.makedirs(LOG_DIR, exist_ok=True)  # Create Logs directory if missing
LOG_FILE = os.path.join(LOG_DIR, "SOC_RTs_Log.txt")

logging.basicConfig(filename=LOG_FILE, format='%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s', level=logging.INFO)

# 🔧 RT API Configuration
RT_URL = "https://rt.marchex.com/REST/1.0"
RT_USER = "socbot"
RT_PASS = "securepass"
RT_QUEUE = "SOC Alerts"  # Adjust if necessary

# ✅ Keywords used to identify a cleared alert
CLEAR_KEYWORDS = ["cleared", "alert cleared", "resolved", "no further action needed"]


def get_rt_session():
    """Establishes an RT API session."""
    tracker = rt.Rt(RT_URL, RT_USER, RT_PASS)
    if tracker.login():
        logging.info("✅ Successfully authenticated with RT.")
        return tracker
    else:
        logging.error("❌ Failed to authenticate with RT.")
        return None


def get_open_tickets(tracker):
    """Fetches open alert tickets from RT."""
    logging.info("🔍 Fetching open alert tickets from RT...")
    
    try:
        tickets = tracker.search(queue=RT_QUEUE, raw_query="Status = 'open'")
        logging.info(f"✅ Found {len(tickets)} open alert tickets.")
        return tickets
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"❌ Error retrieving RT tickets: {e}")
        return []


def is_alert_cleared(tracker, ticket_id):
    """Checks if the latest comment on an RT ticket indicates the alert is cleared."""
    logging.info(f"🔎 Checking RT ticket #{ticket_id} for cleared alert status...")

    try:
        history = tracker.get_ticket_history(ticket_id)
        if not history:
            logging.info(f"⚠️ No history found for RT ticket #{ticket_id}. Assuming NOT cleared.")
            return False
        
        latest_comment = history[-1]["Content"].strip().lower() if history else ""
        if any(keyword in latest_comment for keyword in CLEAR_KEYWORDS):
            logging.info(f"✅ Alert in RT ticket #{ticket_id} is cleared.")
            return True
        else:
            logging.info(f"❌ Alert in RT ticket #{ticket_id} is NOT cleared.")
            return False
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"❌ Error checking alert status for RT ticket #{ticket_id}: {e}")
        return False


def close_ticket(tracker, ticket_id):
    """Resolves and closes an RT ticket if alert is cleared."""
    logging.info(f"🔒 Resolving RT ticket #{ticket_id}...")

    try:
        tracker.edit_ticket(ticket_id, Status="resolved")
        tracker.comment_on_ticket(ticket_id, "✅ Alert has been cleared. Auto-closing ticket.")
        logging.info(f"✅ RT ticket #{ticket_id} has been successfully closed.")
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"❌ Error closing RT ticket #{ticket_id}: {e}")


def process_tickets():
    """Processes all open RT tickets and closes those with cleared alerts."""
    tracker = get_rt_session()
    if not tracker:
        logging.error("❌ Unable to proceed without RT authentication.")
        return

    tickets = get_open_tickets(tracker)

    if not tickets:
        logging.info("✅ No open RT tickets found. Exiting...")
        return

    for ticket in tickets:
        ticket_id = ticket["id"]
        
        if is_alert_cleared(tracker, ticket_id):
            close_ticket(tracker, ticket_id)

    logging.info("✅ All cleared RT tickets processed successfully!")


if __name__ == "__main__":
    process_tickets()




heres the close_cleared_rts.py script it should also not contain any gui components and should also align with Matts vision of simplicity, maintainability and clarity,
"""
RT API Helper Module
-----------------------------------------
This script provides helper functions to interact with the RT (Request Tracker) API.

🛠️ Features:
- Adds comments to RT tickets
- Logs all interactions in Logs/SOC_RT_API_Log.txt
✅ Designed for easy integration with SOC scripts.
"""

import requests
import logging
import os

# ✅ Setup Logging in Logs Directory
BASE_DIR = os.path.dirname(os.path.abspath(__file__))  # Get script directory
LOG_DIR = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "Logs")
os.makedirs(LOG_DIR, exist_ok=True)  # Create Logs directory if missing
LOG_FILE = os.path.join(LOG_DIR, "SOC_RT_API_Log.txt")

logging.basicConfig(filename=LOG_FILE, format='%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s', level=logging.INFO)

# 🔧 RT API Configuration
RT_URL = "https://rt.marchex.com/REST/1.0"
RT_USER = "socbot"
RT_PASS = "securepass"


def add_comment(ticket_number, comment):
    """
    Adds a comment to an RT ticket.

    Args:
        ticket_number (str): The RT ticket number.
        comment (str): The comment content to be added.
    
    Returns:
        bool: True if successful, False otherwise.
    """

    if not ticket_number:
        logging.warning("⚠️ No RT ticket number provided. Skipping comment.")
        return False

    if not comment.strip():
        logging.warning(f"⚠️ Empty comment for RT Ticket #{ticket_number}. Skipping.")
        return False

    logging.info(f"📝 Attempting to comment on RT Ticket #{ticket_number}...")

    url = f"{RT_URL}/ticket/{ticket_number}/comment"
    data = {"content": comment}

    try:
        response = requests.post(url, auth=(RT_USER, RT_PASS), data=data, timeout=10)

        if response.status_code == 200:
            logging.info(f"✅ Successfully commented on RT Ticket #{ticket_number}")
            return True
        else:
            logging.error(f"❌ Failed to comment on RT Ticket #{ticket_number}. Response: {response.text}")
            return False

    except requests.exceptions.RequestException as e:
        logging.error(f"❌ Request error while commenting on RT Ticket #{ticket_number}: {e}")
        return False


def get_ticket_details(ticket_number):
    """
    Retrieves details of an RT ticket.

    Args:
        ticket_number (str): The RT ticket number.
    
    Returns:
        dict: Ticket details if successful, None otherwise.
    """

    if not ticket_number:
        logging.warning("⚠️ No RT ticket number provided. Skipping request.")
        return None

    logging.info(f"📋 Fetching details for RT Ticket #{ticket_number}...")

    url = f"{RT_URL}/ticket/{ticket_number}/show"

    try:
        response = requests.get(url, auth=(RT_USER, RT_PASS), timeout=10)

        if response.status_code == 200:
            ticket_data = response.text
            logging.info(f"✅ Successfully retrieved details for RT Ticket #{ticket_number}")
            return ticket_data
        else:
            logging.error(f"❌ Failed to retrieve RT Ticket #{ticket_number}. Response: {response.text}")
            return None

    except requests.exceptions.RequestException as e:
        logging.error(f"❌ Request error while fetching RT Ticket #{ticket_number}: {e}")
        return None

"""
SOC Access Management Tool (CLI First, GUI Optional)
----------------------------------------------------
Provides a simple interface for SOC access management:
- Check User Access
- Grant User Access
- Remove User Access
- Clear RT Ticket Queue

🛠️ Designed for **command-line operation** with an optional GUI.
✅ Aligned with Matt's goal: **simplicity, maintainability, and clarity**.
"""

import sys
import os
import subprocess

# Set up base directories
BASE_DIR = os.path.dirname(os.path.abspath(__file__))  # Get the script's directory
UTILS_DIR = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "Utils")  # Locate utilities directory
sys.path.append(UTILS_DIR)  # Add Utils to Python path for importing shared modules

from rt_api import add_comment  # Import RT API functionality

# Define paths to access management scripts
CHECK_ACCESS_SCRIPT = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "CheckAccess", "checkaccess.py")
GRANT_ACCESS_SCRIPT = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "GrantAccess", "grantaccess.py")
REMOVE_ACCESS_SCRIPT = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "RemoveAccess", "separation.py")
CLEAR_RT_SCRIPT = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "close_cleared_rts.py")

# CLI Mode: Provide usage instructions
if len(sys.argv) > 1:
    print("\nSOC Access Management Tool (CLI First, GUI Optional)")
    print("====================================================")
    print("Usage:")
    print("  python soctool.py   # Starts the GUI (optional)")
    print("  python checkaccess.py <ldap_user> <ldap_pass> <target_user> --rt_ticket <ticket_number>")
    print("  python grantaccess.py <ldap_user> <ldap_pass> <target_user> --mock --rt_ticket <ticket_number>")
    print("  python separation.py <ldap_user> <ldap_pass> <target_user> --mock --rt_ticket <ticket_number>")
    print("  python close_cleared_rts.py   # Clears resolved RT tickets")
    sys.exit()  # Exit CLI mode

# GUI Dependencies (Optional)
try:
    import tkinter as tk
    from tkinter import messagebox
except ImportError:
    print("Tkinter is not installed. Run scripts via CLI instead.")
    sys.exit()

def open_access_window(action, script_path, show_mock_mode=True):
    """
    Opens a GUI window for user access management.

    Args:
        action (str): "Check", "Grant", or "Remove" (determines window title and action).
        script_path (str): Path to the corresponding script.
        show_mock_mode (bool): Whether to show the mock mode checkbox (only for Grant and Remove).
    """

    action_window = tk.Toplevel(root)
    action_window.title(f"SOC - {action} Access")
    action_window.geometry("500x525")

    tk.Label(action_window, text=f"{action} User Access", font=("Arial", 14, "bold")).pack(pady=10)

    # LDAP Credentials
    tk.Label(action_window, text="Enter your LDAP username:").pack()
    ldap_entry = tk.Entry(action_window, width=40)
    ldap_entry.pack(pady=5)

    tk.Label(action_window, text="Enter your LDAP password:").pack()
    ldap_pass_entry = tk.Entry(action_window, width=40, show="*")  # Hide password input
    ldap_pass_entry.pack(pady=5)

    # Target User
    tk.Label(action_window, text=f"Enter LDAP username to {action.lower()} access for:").pack()
    target_user_entry = tk.Entry(action_window, width=40)
    target_user_entry.pack(pady=5)

    # RT Ticket Number (Optional)
    tk.Label(action_window, text="Enter RT Ticket Number (Optional):").pack()
    rt_ticket_entry = tk.Entry(action_window, width=40)
    rt_ticket_entry.pack(pady=5)

    # Mock Mode Toggle (only shown for Grant and Remove)
    mock_mode = tk.BooleanVar(value=True)
    if show_mock_mode:
        tk.Checkbutton(action_window, text="Enable Mock Mode", variable=mock_mode).pack()

    # Log Display
    tk.Label(action_window, text="Logs:").pack()
    log_area = tk.Text(action_window, width=60, height=10)
    log_area.pack(pady=5)

    def execute_action():
        """Executes the selected access action script."""
        ldap_user = ldap_entry.get().strip()
        ldap_pass = ldap_pass_entry.get().strip()
        target_user = target_user_entry.get().strip()
        rt_ticket = rt_ticket_entry.get().strip()
        mock_flag = "--mock" if show_mock_mode and mock_mode.get() else ""

        # Ensure required fields are filled
        if not ldap_user or not ldap_pass or not target_user:
            messagebox.showerror("Error", "All fields are required except RT Ticket.")
            return

        log_area.insert(tk.END, f"🚀 Running {action} script for {target_user}...\n")
        log_area.see(tk.END)

        def execute():
            try:
                result = subprocess.run(
                    ["python", script_path, ldap_user, ldap_pass, target_user, rt_ticket, mock_flag],
                    capture_output=True, text=True
                )
                log_area.insert(tk.END, result.stdout + "\n")
                log_area.insert(tk.END, result.stderr + "\n")
            except subprocess.CalledProcessError as e:
                log_area.insert(tk.END, f"❌ Error: {e.stderr}\n")

        # Run script in a separate thread to prevent UI freezing
        import threading
        threading.Thread(target=execute, daemon=True).start()

    tk.Button(action_window, text="Execute", command=execute_action, font=("Arial", 12), width=20).pack(pady=10)


# GUI Window Setup
root = tk.Tk()
root.title("SOC Access Management")
root.geometry("400x350")
root.resizable(False, False)

# Header
tk.Label(root, text="SOC Access Management", font=("Arial", 14, "bold")).pack(pady=20)

# Buttons to trigger scripts
tk.Button(root, text="Check User Access", font=("Arial", 12),
          command=lambda: open_access_window("Check", CHECK_ACCESS_SCRIPT, show_mock_mode=False), width=25, height=2).pack(pady=5)

tk.Button(root, text="Grant User Access", font=("Arial", 12),
          command=lambda: open_access_window("Grant", GRANT_ACCESS_SCRIPT, show_mock_mode=True), width=25, height=2).pack(pady=5)

tk.Button(root, text="Remove User Access", font=("Arial", 12),
          command=lambda: open_access_window("Remove", REMOVE_ACCESS_SCRIPT, show_mock_mode=True), width=25, height=2).pack(pady=5)

tk.Button(root, text="Clear RT Queue", font=("Arial", 12),
          command=lambda: subprocess.run(["python", CLEAR_RT_SCRIPT]), width=25, height=2).pack(pady=5)

# Start GUI
root.mainloop()

def open_clear_rt_window():
    """
    Opens a GUI window to display RT queue clearing process in real-time.
    """

    rt_window = tk.Toplevel(root)
    rt_window.title("Clearing RT Queue")
    rt_window.geometry("500x400")

    tk.Label(rt_window, text="Processing RT Queue...", font=("Arial", 14, "bold")).pack(pady=10)

    # Log Display
    log_area = scrolledtext.ScrolledText(rt_window, width=60, height=15)
    log_area.pack(pady=5)

    def execute_clear_rt():
        """
        Executes the RT queue clearing script and updates the GUI log.
        """
        try:
            process = subprocess.Popen(
                ["python", CLEAR_RT_SCRIPT],
                stdout=subprocess.PIPE,
                stderr=subprocess.PIPE,
                text=True
            )

            # Capture real-time output from the script
            for line in iter(process.stdout.readline, ""):
                log_area.insert(tk.END, line)
                log_area.see(tk.END)

            # Capture any errors
            for line in iter(process.stderr.readline, ""):
                log_area.insert(tk.END, f"❌ ERROR: {line}")
                log_area.see(tk.END)

        except Exception as e:
            log_area.insert(tk.END, f"❌ Error running RT queue clear script: {e}\n")

    # Run script in a separate thread to prevent UI freezing
    threading.Thread(target=execute_clear_rt, daemon=True).start()

def open_clear_rt_window():
    """
    Opens a GUI window to display RT queue clearing process in real-time.
    """

    rt_window = tk.Toplevel(root)
    rt_window.title("Clearing RT Queue")
    rt_window.geometry("600x400")

    tk.Label(rt_window, text="Processing RT Queue...", font=("Arial", 14, "bold")).pack(pady=10)

    # Log Display
    log_area = scrolledtext.ScrolledText(rt_window, width=70, height=15)
    log_area.pack(pady=5)

    def execute_clear_rt():
        """
        Executes the RT queue clearing script and updates the GUI log in real-time.
        """
        try:
            process = subprocess.Popen(
                ["python", CLEAR_RT_SCRIPT],
                stdout=subprocess.PIPE,
                stderr=subprocess.PIPE,
                text=True,
                bufsize=1
            )

            # Read stdout and stderr line by line
            for line in iter(process.stdout.readline, ""):
                log_area.insert(tk.END, f"✅ {line}")
                log_area.see(tk.END)

            for line in iter(process.stderr.readline, ""):
                log_area.insert(tk.END, f"❌ ERROR: {line}")
                log_area.see(tk.END)

            process.stdout.close()
            process.stderr.close()
            process.wait()

            log_area.insert(tk.END, "\n✔ RT Queue Processing Complete!\n")

        except Exception as e:
            log_area.insert(tk.END, f"❌ Error running RT queue clear script: {e}\n")

    # Run script in a separate thread to prevent UI freezing
    threading.Thread(target=execute_clear_rt, daemon=True).start()

# GUI Window Setup
root = tk.Tk()
root.title("SOC Access Management")
root.geometry("400x350")
root.resizable(False, False)

# Header
tk.Label(root, text="SOC Access Management", font=("Arial", 14, "bold")).pack(pady=20)

# Buttons to trigger scripts

          command=lambda: subprocess.run(["python", CLEAR_RT_SCRIPT]), width=25, height=2).pack(pady=5)

# Start GUI
root.mainloop()
