before we move on id like to reiterate Matt's guidelines: maintainability, simplicity, and clarity. and also because this script is only to be CHECKING for access a MOCK mode is not needed, id also like to test this script fully before moving on to the next one.
check_adtrack.py seems to be importing a script called "secret.py" from the lib directory in the original repo, i copied this directory into my Soctool directory to use with my new restructuring but since check_adtrack.py is calling secret id like to take a look at it and update it for use, id also like you to explain to me what it does and how and why check_adtrack uses it




"""
SOC Access Check Script (CLI Only)
-----------------------------------------
Checks a user's access across multiple SOC systems.

🛠️ Features:
- Runs system-specific access checks via external scripts.
- Logs results in Logs/SOC_Access_Log.txt.
- Automatically updates an RT ticket (if provided).
✅ **Designed for CLI operation only.** GUI is handled separately in soctool.py.
"""

import argparse
import logging
import os
import subprocess
import sys
from datetime import datetime

# Ensure Utils is accessible for rt_api.py
BASE_DIR = os.path.dirname(os.path.abspath(__file__))  # Get current script location
UTILS_DIR = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "..", "Utils")  # Locate Utils folder
sys.path.append(UTILS_DIR)  # Add to system path

from rt_api import add_comment  # Import RT API functionality

# ✅ Define directory for system-specific check scripts
SYSTEMS_DIR = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "Systems")

# ✅ Ensure logs are stored in a Logs folder
LOG_DIR = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "..", "Logs")
os.makedirs(LOG_DIR, exist_ok=True)  # Create Logs directory if missing
LOG_FILE = os.path.join(LOG_DIR, "SOC_Access_Log.txt")

# ✅ Configure logging format
logging.basicConfig(filename=LOG_FILE, format='%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s', level=logging.INFO)

def check_access(username, ldap_user, ldap_pass, rt_ticket=None):
    """
    Checks a user's access across multiple SOC systems.

    Args:
        username (str): The LDAP username to check.
        ldap_user (str): The SOC user's LDAP username.
        ldap_pass (str): The SOC user's LDAP password.
        rt_ticket (str, optional): RT ticket number for logging results.

    Returns:
        None
    """

    timestamp = datetime.now().strftime("%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S")
    logging.info(f"===== START: {timestamp} - Checking Access for {username} =====")

    results = []  # Store access check results

    # Loop through all scripts in the Systems directory
    for script in os.listdir(SYSTEMS_DIR):
        if script.startswith("check_") and script.endswith(".py"):
            system_name = script.replace("check_", "").replace(".py", "").capitalize()
            script_path = os.path.join(SYSTEMS_DIR, script)

            try:
                # Run the system-specific check script
                result = subprocess.run(
                    ["python", script_path, username],
                    capture_output=True,
                    text=True
                )

                # Append the result to the list
                results.append(f"✅ {system_name}: {result.stdout.strip()}")
                logging.info(f"{system_name} - {result.stdout.strip()}")

            except Exception as e:
                results.append(f"❌ {system_name}: Error running script - {e}")
                logging.error(f"Error running {system_name} script: {e}")

    # ✅ Summarize results
    summary = f"\n🔹 Access check for {username} at {timestamp}\n" + "\n".join(results)

    # ✅ Log results to an RT ticket if provided
    if rt_ticket:
        add_comment(rt_ticket, summary)

    logging.info(f"===== END: {timestamp} - Check Completed for {username} =====\n")

    # ✅ Print summary to CLI
    print(summary)


if __name__ == "__main__":
    # ✅ CLI Mode - Parse Command Line Arguments
    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(description="Check user access across SOC systems.")
    parser.add_argument("ldap_user", help="Your LDAP username")
    parser.add_argument("ldap_pass", help="Your LDAP password")
    parser.add_argument("username", help="LDAP username of the user to check")
    parser.add_argument("--rt_ticket", help="RT Ticket number for documentation", default=None)

    # Parse CLI arguments
    args = parser.parse_args()

    # Run the access check function
    check_access(args.username, args.ldap_user, args.ldap_pass, args.rt_ticket)




import logging
import sys
import os

"""
USAGE:
------

> import Secret
> user = get_secret('<USER_KEY>')
> pass = get_secret('<PASS_KEY>')


Ex:
> test = get_secret('_SAFE_TEST_PASS')
> print "Password is: " + test

Password is: SafeTestPassword!

"""

SECRETS = {}
SECRET_FILE = ''

if 'SECRET_FILE' in os.environ and os.path.isfile(os.environ['SECRET_FILE']):
	SECRET_FILE = os.environ['SECRET_FILE']
elif 'HOME' in os.environ and os.path.isfile(os.environ['HOME']+'/conf/secret.conf'):
	SECRET_FILE = os.environ['HOME']+'/conf/secret.conf'
else:
	SECRET_FILE = '/site/socbot/conf/secret.conf'


def load_secrets():
	try:
		with open(SECRET_FILE, 'r') as f:
			for line in f:
				try:
					(key,val) = line.split('=',1)
				except:
					continue
				SECRETS[key] = val.rstrip()
	except IOError:
		raise IOError("Cannot open {} (Secret file).".format(SECRET_FILE))

def get_secret(key):
	if not SECRETS:
		load_secrets()
	
	if key in SECRETS:
		return SECRETS[key]
	else:
		raise Exception("Secret named '{}' does not exist in '{}'!".format(key, SECRET_FILE))

def test():
	import pprint
	pprint.pprint(SECRETS)
before moving on lets look at soctool.py checkaccess, check_adtrack.py and secret and let make sure everything looks good and meets Matt's guidelines: maintainability, simplicity, and clarity.




"""
SOC Access Management Tool (CLI First, GUI Optional)
----------------------------------------------------
Provides a simple interface for SOC access management:
- Check User Access
- Grant User Access
- Remove User Access
- Clear RT Ticket Queue

🛠️ Designed for **command-line operation** with an optional GUI.
✅ Aligned with Matt's goal: **simplicity, maintainability, and clarity**.
"""

import sys
import os
import subprocess
import threading

# GUI Dependencies (Optional)
try:
    import tkinter as tk
    from tkinter import messagebox, scrolledtext
except ImportError:
    print("Tkinter is not installed. Run scripts via CLI instead.")
    sys.exit()

# Set up base directories
BASE_DIR = os.path.dirname(os.path.abspath(__file__))  # Get the script's directory
UTILS_DIR = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "Utils")  # Locate utilities directory
sys.path.append(UTILS_DIR)  # Add Utils to Python path for importing shared modules

from rt_api import add_comment  # Import RT API functionality

# Define paths to access management scripts
CHECK_ACCESS_SCRIPT = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "CheckAccess", "checkaccess.py")
GRANT_ACCESS_SCRIPT = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "GrantAccess", "grantaccess.py")
REMOVE_ACCESS_SCRIPT = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "RemoveAccess", "separation.py")
CLEAR_RT_SCRIPT = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "close_cleared_rts.py")

# CLI Mode: Provide usage instructions
if len(sys.argv) > 1:
    print("\nSOC Access Management Tool (CLI First, GUI Optional)")
    print("====================================================")
    print("Usage:")
    print("  python soctool.py   # Starts the GUI (optional)")
    print("  python checkaccess.py <ldap_user> <ldap_pass> <target_user> --rt_ticket <ticket_number>")
    print("  python grantaccess.py <ldap_user> <ldap_pass> <target_user> --mock --rt_ticket <ticket_number>")
    print("  python separation.py <ldap_user> <ldap_pass> <target_user> --mock --rt_ticket <ticket_number>")
    print("  python close_cleared_rts.py   # Clears resolved RT tickets")
    sys.exit()  # Exit CLI mode


def open_access_window(action, script_path, show_mock_mode=True):
    """
    Opens a GUI window for user access management.

    Args:
        action (str): "Check", "Grant", or "Remove" (determines window title and action).
        script_path (str): Path to the corresponding script.
        show_mock_mode (bool): Whether to show the mock mode checkbox (only for Grant and Remove).
    """

    action_window = tk.Toplevel(root)
    action_window.title(f"SOC - {action} Access")
    action_window.geometry("500x525")

    tk.Label(action_window, text=f"{action} User Access", font=("Arial", 14, "bold")).pack(pady=10)

    # LDAP Credentials
    tk.Label(action_window, text="Enter your LDAP username:").pack()
    ldap_entry = tk.Entry(action_window, width=40)
    ldap_entry.pack(pady=5)

    tk.Label(action_window, text="Enter your LDAP password:").pack()
    ldap_pass_entry = tk.Entry(action_window, width=40, show="*")  # Hide password input
    ldap_pass_entry.pack(pady=5)

    # Target User
    tk.Label(action_window, text=f"Enter LDAP username to {action.lower()} access for:").pack()
    target_user_entry = tk.Entry(action_window, width=40)
    target_user_entry.pack(pady=5)

    # RT Ticket Number (Optional)
    tk.Label(action_window, text="Enter RT Ticket Number (Optional):").pack()
    rt_ticket_entry = tk.Entry(action_window, width=40)
    rt_ticket_entry.pack(pady=5)

    # Mock Mode Toggle (only shown for Grant and Remove)
    mock_mode = tk.BooleanVar(value=True)
    if show_mock_mode:
        tk.Checkbutton(action_window, text="Enable Mock Mode", variable=mock_mode).pack()

    # Log Display
    tk.Label(action_window, text="Logs:").pack()
    log_area = tk.Text(action_window, width=60, height=10)
    log_area.pack(pady=5)

    def execute_action():
        """Executes the selected access action script."""
        ldap_user = ldap_entry.get().strip()
        ldap_pass = ldap_pass_entry.get().strip()
        target_user = target_user_entry.get().strip()
        rt_ticket = rt_ticket_entry.get().strip()
        mock_flag = "--mock" if show_mock_mode and mock_mode.get() else ""

        # Ensure required fields are filled
        if not ldap_user or not ldap_pass or not target_user:
            messagebox.showerror("Error", "All fields are required except RT Ticket.")
            return

        log_area.insert(tk.END, f"🚀 Running {action} script for {target_user}...\n")
        log_area.see(tk.END)

        def execute():
            try:
                result = subprocess.run(
                    ["python", script_path, ldap_user, ldap_pass, target_user, rt_ticket, mock_flag],
                    capture_output=True, text=True
                )
                log_area.insert(tk.END, result.stdout + "\n")
                log_area.insert(tk.END, result.stderr + "\n")
            except subprocess.CalledProcessError as e:
                log_area.insert(tk.END, f"❌ Error: {e.stderr}\n")

        # Run script in a separate thread to prevent UI freezing
        import threading
        threading.Thread(target=execute, daemon=True).start()

    tk.Button(action_window, text="Execute", command=execute_action, font=("Arial", 12), width=20).pack(pady=10)

def open_clear_rt_window():
    """
    Opens a GUI window to display RT queue clearing process in real-time.
    """

    rt_window = tk.Toplevel(root)
    rt_window.title("Clearing RT Queue")
    rt_window.geometry("600x400")

    tk.Label(rt_window, text="Processing RT Queue...", font=("Arial", 14, "bold")).pack(pady=10)

    # Log Display
    log_area = scrolledtext.ScrolledText(rt_window, width=70, height=15)
    log_area.pack(pady=5)

    def execute_clear_rt():
        """
        Executes the RT queue clearing script and updates the GUI log in real-time.
        """
        try:
            process = subprocess.Popen(
                ["python", CLEAR_RT_SCRIPT],
                stdout=subprocess.PIPE,
                stderr=subprocess.PIPE,
                text=True,
                encoding="utf-8",  # ✅ Ensure UTF-8 is used
                bufsize=1
            )

            # Read stdout and stderr line by line
            for line in iter(process.stdout.readline, ""):
                log_area.insert(tk.END, f"✅ {line}")
                log_area.see(tk.END)

            for line in iter(process.stderr.readline, ""):
                log_area.insert(tk.END, f"❌ ERROR: {line}")
                log_area.see(tk.END)

            process.stdout.close()
            process.stderr.close()
            process.wait()

            log_area.insert(tk.END, "\n✔ RT Queue Processing Complete!\n")

        except Exception as e:
            log_area.insert(tk.END, f"❌ Error running RT queue clear script: {e}\n")

    # Run script in a separate thread to prevent UI freezing
    threading.Thread(target=execute_clear_rt, daemon=True).start()

# GUI Window Setup
root = tk.Tk()
root.title("SOC Access Management")
root.geometry("400x350")
root.resizable(False, False)

# Header
tk.Label(root, text="SOC Access Management", font=("Arial", 14, "bold")).pack(pady=20)

# Buttons to trigger scripts
tk.Button(root, text="Check User Access", font=("Arial", 12),
          command=lambda: open_access_window("Check", CHECK_ACCESS_SCRIPT, show_mock_mode=False), width=25, height=2).pack(pady=5)

tk.Button(root, text="Grant User Access", font=("Arial", 12),
          command=lambda: open_access_window("Grant", GRANT_ACCESS_SCRIPT, show_mock_mode=True), width=25, height=2).pack(pady=5)

tk.Button(root, text="Remove User Access", font=("Arial", 12),
          command=lambda: open_access_window("Remove", REMOVE_ACCESS_SCRIPT, show_mock_mode=True), width=25, height=2).pack(pady=5)

tk.Button(root, text="Clear RT Queue", font=("Arial", 12),
          command=lambda: open_clear_rt_window(), width=25, height=2).pack(pady=5)

# Start GUI
root.mainloop()




"""
SOC Access Check Script (CLI Only)
-----------------------------------------
Checks a user's access across multiple SOC systems.

🛠️ Features:
- Runs system-specific access checks via external scripts.
- Logs results in Logs/SOC_Access_Log.txt.
- Automatically updates an RT ticket (if provided).
✅ **Designed for CLI operation only.** GUI is handled separately in soctool.py.
"""

import argparse
import logging
import os
import subprocess
import sys
from datetime import datetime

# Ensure Utils is accessible for rt_api.py
BASE_DIR = os.path.dirname(os.path.abspath(__file__))  # Get current script location
UTILS_DIR = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "..", "Utils")  # Locate Utils folder
sys.path.append(UTILS_DIR)  # Add to system path

from rt_api import add_comment  # Import RT API functionality

# ✅ Define directory for system-specific check scripts
SYSTEMS_DIR = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "Systems")

# ✅ Ensure logs are stored in a Logs folder
LOG_DIR = os.path.join(BASE_DIR, "..", "Logs")
os.makedirs(LOG_DIR, exist_ok=True)  # Create Logs directory if missing
LOG_FILE = os.path.join(LOG_DIR, "SOC_Access_Log.txt")

# ✅ Configure logging format
logging.basicConfig(filename=LOG_FILE, format='%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s', level=logging.INFO)

def check_access(username, ldap_user, ldap_pass, rt_ticket=None):
    """
    Checks a user's access across multiple SOC systems.

    Args:
        username (str): The LDAP username to check.
        ldap_user (str): The SOC user's LDAP username.
        ldap_pass (str): The SOC user's LDAP password.
        rt_ticket (str, optional): RT ticket number for logging results.

    Returns:
        None
    """

    timestamp = datetime.now().strftime("%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S")
    logging.info(f"===== START: {timestamp} - Checking Access for {username} =====")

    results = []  # Store access check results

    # Loop through all scripts in the Systems directory
    for script in os.listdir(SYSTEMS_DIR):
        if script.startswith("check_") and script.endswith(".py"):
            system_name = script.replace("check_", "").replace(".py", "").capitalize()
            script_path = os.path.join(SYSTEMS_DIR, script)

            try:
                # Run the system-specific check script
                result = subprocess.run(
                    ["python", script_path, username],
                    capture_output=True,
                    text=True
                )

                # Append the result to the list
                results.append(f"✅ {system_name}: {result.stdout.strip()}")
                logging.info(f"{system_name} - {result.stdout.strip()}")

            except Exception as e:
                results.append(f"❌ {system_name}: Error running script - {e}")
                logging.error(f"Error running {system_name} script: {e}")

    # ✅ Summarize results
    summary = f"\n🔹 Access check for {username} at {timestamp}\n" + "\n".join(results)

    # ✅ Log results to an RT ticket if provided
    if rt_ticket:
        add_comment(rt_ticket, summary)

    logging.info(f"===== END: {timestamp} - Check Completed for {username} =====\n")

    # ✅ Print summary to CLI
    print(summary)


if __name__ == "__main__":
    # ✅ CLI Mode - Parse Command Line Arguments
    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(description="Check user access across SOC systems.")
    parser.add_argument("ldap_user", help="Your LDAP username")
    parser.add_argument("ldap_pass", help="Your LDAP password")
    parser.add_argument("username", help="LDAP username of the user to check")
    parser.add_argument("--rt_ticket", help="RT Ticket number for documentation", default=None)

    # Parse CLI arguments
    args = parser.parse_args()

    # Run the access check function
    check_access(args.username, args.ldap_user, args.ldap_pass, args.rt_ticket)




import logging
import psycopg2
import sys
sys.path.append('../../../../lib/python')
import secret

# ✅ Setup logging
logging.basicConfig(
    format="%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s",
    level=logging.INFO
)

# ✅ Database configuration
DB_CONFIG = {
    "dbname": "adtrack_ro",
    "host": "vspool.som1.marchex.com",
    "port": 5432,
    "user": secret.get_secret("_ADTRACK_DB_USER"),
    "password": secret.get_secret("_ADTRACK_DB_PASS")
}

def get_db_connection():
    """Establish a database connection to AdTrack."""
    try:
        return psycopg2.connect(**DB_CONFIG)
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"❌ Database connection failed: {e}")
        return None

def check_adtrack_access(user, vendor_email=None):
    """Check if a user has AdTrack UI access."""
    search_param = vendor_email or f"{user}@marchex.com"

    conn = get_db_connection()
    if not conn:
        return None

    query = "SELECT email FROM at_user WHERE email ILIKE %s AND status != 'disabled'"
    try:
        with conn.cursor() as cur:
            cur.execute(query, (search_param,))
            result = cur.fetchall()

        conn.close()
        return [row[0] for row in result] if result else None

    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"❌ Database query failed: {e}")
        return None

def main():
    """Run the script for checking AdTrack UI access."""
    sep_list = input("Enter LDAP user(s) to check (comma-separated): ").split(",")
    is_vendor = input("Is this user a vendor? (Yes/No): ").strip().lower()
    vendor_email = input("Enter vendor email address: ") if is_vendor == "yes" else None

    for user in sep_list:
        user = user.strip()
        access = check_adtrack_access(user, vendor_email)

        if access:
            logging.info(f"✅ {user} has AdTrack UI access: {access}")
        else:
            logging.info(f"❌ {user} does NOT have AdTrack UI access.")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()




import logging
import os

# ✅ Setup logging
logging.basicConfig(
    format="%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s",
    level=logging.INFO
)

# ✅ Define the default secret file location
SECRET_FILE = os.getenv("SECRET_FILE", "/site/socbot/conf/secret.conf")
SECRETS = {}

def load_secrets():
    """Load secrets from the specified secret file into memory."""
    if not os.path.isfile(SECRET_FILE):
        logging.error(f"❌ Secret file '{SECRET_FILE}' not found!")
        return

    try:
        with open(SECRET_FILE, "r") as f:
            for line in f:
                if "=" in line:
                    key, val = line.strip().split("=", 1)
                    SECRETS[key] = val

        logging.info("✅ Secrets successfully loaded.")

    except IOError as e:
        logging.error(f"❌ Failed to read secret file: {e}")

def get_secret(key):
    """Retrieve a secret value by its key."""
    if not SECRETS:
        load_secrets()  # Load secrets if they are not already in memory

    secret_value = SECRETS.get(key)
    if secret_value:
        return secret_value
    else:
        logging.warning(f"⚠️ Secret '{key}' not found in '{SECRET_FILE}'")
        return None  # Return None instead of raising an error

# ✅ Testing function (optional for debugging)
def test():
    """Print all loaded secrets (For debugging only - do NOT use in production)."""
    import pprint
    pprint.pprint(SECRETS)

# ✅ Auto-load secrets when script is imported
load_secrets()

<Option crontab>

	Command Exec 0 0 ln -s ${marchexbase}/conf/socbot.cron /etc/cron.d/${name}
	Command Exec 0 0 chown root:root ${marchexbase}/conf/socbot.cron
	Command Exec 0 0 chmod 600 ${marchexbase}/conf/socbot.cron
</Option>

<Option fcrontab>
	# requires fcron to be installed
	Command Exec 0 0 rm -f /usr/local/var/spool/fcron/${name}.*
	Command Exec 0 0 ln -s ${marchexbase}/conf/socbot.fcron /usr/local/var/spool/fcron/${name}.orig
	Command Exec 0 0 chown fcron:fcron ${marchexbase}/conf/socbot.fcron
	Command Exec 0 0 chmod 640 ${marchexbase}/conf/socbot.fcron
	Command Exec 0 0 sudo -u socbot fcrontab -z
</Option>

<Option pip>
	Command Exec 0 0 pip install --upgrade pip
	Command Exec 0 0 sudo -iu socbot pip install --user --upgrade --requirement=${marchexbase}/requirements.txt --build-directory=/tmp/build
</Option>

<Source production>
	Mode		Alike
	<Commands>
		Command	Rsync ${marchexbase} nodelete-alike
		# Escrow
		Command Exec 0 0 chown socbot:805 ${escrowfiles}
		Command Exec 0 0 chmod 440 ${escrowfiles}
		Command Descrow ${name} ${escrowfiles} # Looks under <socbot>KEY=VALUE</socbot>
		# END Escrow
		Command ByDefault crontab
		Command ByDefault fcrontab
		Command Option pip
	</Commands>
</Source>

DB_CONFIG = {
    "dbname": "adtrack_ro",
    "host": "vspool.som1.marchex.com",
    "port": 5432,
    "user": secret.get_secret("_ADTRACK_DB_USER"),
    "password": secret.get_secret("_ADTRACK_DB_PASS")
}

def get_db_connection():
    """Establish a database connection to AdTrack."""
    try:
        return psycopg2.connect(**DB_CONFIG)
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"❌ Database connection failed: {e}")
        return None

def check_adtrack_access(user, vendor_email=None):
    """Check if a user has AdTrack UI access."""
    search_param = vendor_email or f"{user}@marchex.com"

    conn = get_db_connection()
    if not conn:
        return None

    query = "SELECT email FROM at_user WHERE email ILIKE %s AND status != 'disabled'"
    try:
        with conn.cursor() as cur:
            cur.execute(query, (search_param,))
            result = cur.fetchall()

        conn.close()
        return [row[0] for row in result] if result else None

    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"❌ Database query failed: {e}")
        return None

def main():
    """Run the script for checking AdTrack UI access."""
    sep_list = input("Enter LDAP user(s) to check (comma-separated): ").split(",")
    is_vendor = input("Is this user a vendor? (Yes/No): ").strip().lower()
    vendor_email = input("Enter vendor email address: ") if is_vendor == "yes" else None

    for user in sep_list:
        user = user.strip()
        access = check_adtrack_access(user, vendor_email)

        if access:
            logging.info(f"✅ {user} has AdTrack UI access: {access}")
        else:
            logging.info(f"❌ {user} does NOT have AdTrack UI access.")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

import logging
import psycopg2
import os
import subprocess

# ✅ Setup logging
logging.basicConfig(
    format="%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s",
    level=logging.INFO
)

def get_dashlane_secret(key):
    """Retrieve secrets from Dashlane CLI."""
    try:
        result = subprocess.run(["dashlane", "vault", "get", key], capture_output=True, text=True)
        return result.stdout.strip() if result.returncode == 0 else None
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"❌ Failed to retrieve {key} from Dashlane: {e}")

import logging
import psycopg2
import os
import subprocess

# ✅ Setup logging
logging.basicConfig(
    format="%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s",
    level=logging.INFO
)

def get_dashlane_note(note_title):
    """Retrieve credentials stored in Dashlane Secure Note."""
    try:
        result = DASHLANE_CLI_PATH = "C:\\Program Files\\DashlaneCLI\\dashlane.exe"
        subprocess.run([DASHLANE_CLI_PATH, "note", note_title], capture_output=True, text=True, check=True)
        lines = result.stdout.strip().split("\n")  # Split into lines
        if len(lines) < 2:
            logging.error("❌ Dashlane note does not contain expected credentials format!")
            return None, None
        return lines[0], lines[1]  # Username, Password
    except subprocess.CalledProcessError as e:
        logging.error(f"❌ Failed to retrieve Dashlane note '{note_title}': {e}")
        return None, None

    "password": ADTRACK_DB_PASS
}

def get_db_connection():
    """Establish a database connection to AdTrack."""
    if not DB_CONFIG["user"] or not DB_CONFIG["password"]:
        logging.error("❌ Database credentials not found in Dashlane! Ensure Dashlane CLI is logged in.")
        return None

    try:
        return psycopg2.connect(**DB_CONFIG)

        return None

import logging
import psycopg2
import os
import subprocess

# ✅ Setup logging
logging.basicConfig(
    format="%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s",
    level=logging.INFO
)

# ✅ Dashlane CLI Path
DASHLANE_CLI_PATH = "C:\\Program Files\\DashlaneCLI\\dashlane.exe"

def get_dashlane_note(note_title):
    """Retrieve credentials stored in Dashlane Secure Note."""
    try:
        result = subprocess.run(
            [DASHLANE_CLI_PATH, "note", note_title],
            capture_output=True,
            text=True,
            check=True
        )

        lines = result.stdout.strip().split("\n")  # Split into lines
        if len(lines) < 2:
            logging.error("❌ Dashlane note does not contain expected credentials format!")
            return None, None

        return lines[0].strip(), lines[1].strip()  # Username, Password

    except subprocess.CalledProcessError as e:
        logging.error(f"❌ Failed to retrieve Dashlane note '{note_title}': {e}")
        return None, None

# ✅ Retrieve database credentials from Dashlane Secure Note
ADTRACK_DB_USER, ADTRACK_DB_PASS = get_dashlane_note("SOC - AdTrack Credentials")

DB_CONFIG = {
    "dbname": "adtrack_ro",
    "host": "vspool.som1.marchex.com",
    "port": 5432,
    "user": ADTRACK_DB_USER,
    "password": ADTRACK_DB_PASS
}

def get_db_connection():
    """Establish a database connection to AdTrack."""
    if not DB_CONFIG["user"] or not DB_CONFIG["password"]:
        logging.error("❌ Database credentials not found in Dashlane! Ensure Dashlane CLI is logged in.")
        return None

    try:
        return psycopg2.connect(**DB_CONFIG)
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"❌ Database connection failed: {e}")
        return None

def check_adtrack_access(user, vendor_email=None):
    """Check if a user has AdTrack UI access."""
    search_param = vendor_email or f"{user}@marchex.com"

    conn = get_db_connection()
    if not conn:
        return None

    query = "SELECT email FROM at_user WHERE email ILIKE %s AND status != 'disabled'"
    try:
        with conn.cursor() as cur:
            cur.execute(query, (search_param,))
            result = cur.fetchall()

        conn.close()
        return [row[0] for row in result] if result else None

    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"❌ Database query failed: {e}")
        return None

def main():
    """Run the script for checking AdTrack UI access."""
    sep_list = input("Enter LDAP user(s) to check (comma-separated): ").split(",")
    is_vendor = input("Is this user a vendor? (Yes/No): ").strip().lower()
    vendor_email = input("Enter vendor email address: ") if is_vendor == "yes" else None

I have been working on updating and debugging a SOC Separation Script written in Python, which automates access removal for departing users at Marchex. The script interacts with LDAP, Request Tracker (RT), and various system APIs.

So far, we have:

Updated the script from Python 2 to Python 3

Converted rt_marchex.py and utils.py to be Python 3-compatible.
Replaced urllib2 with requests and updated print statements.
Resolved Python module import issues

Resolved errors related to missing rt and ldap3 functions.
